      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="List_of_lunar_eclipses_between_-599_and_-500">
        List of lunar eclipses between -599 and -500
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_6th-century_BCE_lunar_eclipses&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: List of lunar eclipses between -599 and -500">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <p>
       There were 255
       <a href="/wiki/Lunar_eclipse" title="Lunar eclipse">
        lunar eclipse
       </a>
       events between -599 and -500 (
       <a href="/wiki/600s_BC_(decade)" title="600s BC (decade)">
        600 BCE
       </a>
       to 501 BCE).
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
